<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотрительный.html>предусмотри́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predusmotrítelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)предусмотри́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)предусмотри́тельней</b>)

***предчувствие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предчувствие.html>предчу́вствие</a> (4687)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čúvstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предчувствие.html>предчу́вствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predčúvstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предчувствие.html>предчу́вствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предчувствие.html>предчу́вствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предчувствие.html>предчу́вствий</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pronounced: predčústvije</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>foreboding, foreshadowing, presentiment, hunch (a premonition; a feeling that something, often of undesirable nature, is going to happen)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предчувствующий.html>предчу́вствующий</a> (9536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***предшествовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предшествовать.html>предше́ствовать</a> (5877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предшествовать.html>предше́ствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predšéstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to precede, to forego, to forerun, to antedate</li></ol>

***предъявить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предъявить.html>предъяви́ть</a> (4883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявить.html>предъяви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predʺjavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to present, to produce, to show
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявить.html>предъяви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predʺjavítʹ</b> bilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show one's ticket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявить.html>предъяви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predʺjavítʹ</b> dokuménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to produce one's papers, to one's documents</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявить.html>предъяви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доказательство.html>доказа́тельства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predʺjavítʹ</b> dokazátelʹstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to produce evidence, to present proofs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make <i>(a demand, request)</i>, to assert <i>(rights)</i></li>
<li>to bring <i>(a lawsuit)</i>, to press, to prefer <i>(an accusation, charge)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">предъявитель</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predʺjavitelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявление.html>предъявле́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predʺjavlénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***предъявляемый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предъявляемый.html>предъявля́емый</a> (9986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявляемый.html>предъявля́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predʺjavljájemyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present passive imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predʺjavljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***предъявлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a> (9986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:являть.html>явля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predʺjavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявить.html>предъяви́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to present, to produce, to show
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predʺjavljátʹ</b> bilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show one's ticket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predʺjavljátʹ</b> dokuménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to produce one's papers, to one's documents</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доказательство.html>доказа́тельства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predʺjavljátʹ</b> dokazátelʹstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to produce evidence, to present proofs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make <i>(a demand, request)</i>, to assert <i>(rights)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предъявлять.html>предъявля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:требование.html>тре́бования</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predʺjavljátʹ</b> bolʹšije trébovanija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make great demands, to demand much</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring <i>(a lawsuit)</i>, to press, to prefer <i>(an accusation, charge)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преждевременный.html>преждевре́менный</a> (13202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прежде.html>пре́жде</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">préžde</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вре́мен-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vrémen-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преждевременный.html>преждевре́менный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preždevrémennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)преждевре́меннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)преждевре́менней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>premature, untimely</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:президентский.html>президе́нтский</a> (5567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:президент.html>президе́нт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prezidént</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:президентский.html>президе́нтский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prezidéntskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> president; presidential

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:презиравший.html>презира́вший</a> (4340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***презирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:презирать.html>презира́ть</a> (4340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ПрѢзьрѢти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">PrĚzĭrĚti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, analyzable as <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prě-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">зьрѭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zĭrjǫ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, akin to today’s <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> . See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zьrěti</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презирать.html>презира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prezirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презреть.html>презре́ть</a></b>) + <i>accusative case</i>
</p>
<ol><li>to despise, to hold in contempt</li>
<li>to scorn, to disdain</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презрение.html>презре́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prezrénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презренный.html>презре́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prezrénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презрительный.html>презри́тельный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prezrítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***презрение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:презрение.html>презре́ние</a> (4557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презреть.html>презре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prezrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презрение.html>презре́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prezrénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презрение.html>презре́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презрение.html>презре́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презрение.html>презре́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contempt, scorn, disdain</li>
<li>defiance</li></ol>

***презрительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:презрительный.html>презри́тельный</a> (4093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презреть.html>презре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prezrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:презрительный.html>презри́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prezrítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>contemptuous, scornful, disdainful <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">showing contempt</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***преимущественно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преимущественно.html>преиму́щественно</a> (5647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преимущественный.html>преиму́щественный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preimúščestvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преимущественно.html>преиму́щественно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preimúščestvenno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>predominantly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a predominant manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>mostly</li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преимущество.html>преиму́щество</a> (3661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:имущество.html>иму́щество</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imúščestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преимущество.html>преиму́щество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preimúščestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преимущество.html>преиму́щества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преимущество.html>преиму́щества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преимущество.html>преиму́ществ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>advantage (any condition, circumstance, opportunity, or means, particularly favorable to success)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преимущество.html>преиму́щество</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>preimúščestvo</b> péred kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">advantage over someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>preference</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Preiskurant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">prix courant</i>.
</p>
